msg:I stayed in two hotels in Shenyang, and Le Meridien was the second one, so I will compare them. Let‚Äôs talk about the comparison with the previous four-star hotel:
Advantages: The location is good. In terms of transportation, it is not far from Shenyang Station and Shenyang North Station. It is adjacent to Taiyuan Street where you can go shopping and not far from the Forbidden City and Middle Street.
     The hotel is decorated in warm colors and looks quite comfortable. The room is spacious. The double bed I stayed in this time was 1.35 meters wide (most hotels are 1.2 meters wide). The heating in the room does not feel very strong, but it is not cold. This is quite accustomed to southerners. The last hotel was too hot.
Disadvantages: The hygiene details are not good. There is a layer of dust on the phone, alarm clock, bedside table, and water bar. This is impossible to happen in the five-star hotels I have stayed in before. The pillows were too high, making it very uncomfortable to sleep on, and the toilet seat was very cold. There were not many breakfast options, and it was worse than staying in a four-star hotel.
  The service is also good, the bellman, front desk, and room service are all very good.
  Finally, I recommend the Chinese restaurant on the 2nd floor which tastes good and the roast duck I ordered was delicious.
